<time>1595734540262< /time><UserId.>118090512074749978397< /UserId.><username>Kelley-Rose Neale<//username>< rating>
5< /rating>
<GmapID>0x80dd29e99dcc18b7:0xb3fa89c900e0d3c8< /GmapID><response>None</response>< review>
I ordered pickup yesterday because I had a craving for their Chow Mein.  When I say I had a craving, I'm saying that I lived 3000 miles away for about 8 years and would wake up missing it.
I ordered for pickup using a third party app and hoped more than anything my order would be correct.  (I'm that girl that will use the "special instructions" section to ask for sides of sauce if the option isn't available... we all know the struggle)
So I'm tired, just excited to have a day off from work (#essential) and I send my  boyfriend in to pick up the order.
He tells me the woman at the counter was so sweet, letting him know sauces were in the bag, etc.

Y'all.

We get home... I open this bag...

Every box is labeled perfectly, with smiley faces drawn onto the grooves in the styrofoam container.  One for my combo plate, one for his.

The sauces, which she labeled and drew a smiley face on, were in their own container.

Then there's this bag of love.
It has a post-it stating "Try Sample dumplings!" with a heart and a smile.

I'm not even kidding, I cried.  It was that.  That's all I needed that day was this extra love they weren't obligated to give, but did so without knowing who they were preparing that meal for.

Long story short, I came for the Chow Mein, and I'm returning for the smiles and dumplings.

Thank you.
2020 sucks, but you guys are the best.</review>

<Name>Ned Gosaynie</Name><text>We came here for lunch on a Sunday and enjoyed traditional and authentic Lebanese fare. Mike, the owner, hails from Zahle, Lebanon, and has been catering and cooking for over 20 years. He went out of his way to make us feel like we were in his home. He offers a full Lebanese menu that includes sandwiches, wraps, combination plates and  manouches. Manouches are pastries with toppings of either a thyme, oregano, olive oil and toasted sesame seed mixture, or a blend of 4 cheeses, or Lahm Bi Ajeen, a mixture of ground beef, tomato, onion and lebanese spices.
We had the zaatar and cheese manouches, along with a pastry stuffed with cooked spinach, onion and lemon juice. We also tried his felafel sandwich, which was delicious and authentic in flavor. I highly recommend you give The Lebanese Oven a try for lunch or dinner sometime soon for something different than the usual.</text></record>

< Text>
Blink and you could miss this cozy little spot, tucked in the back corner of a strip mall -- but don't blink, cos this spot is AMAZING!! Authentic Lebanese flavors (including garlic sauce you'll want to bathe in), with a SoCal twist, including falafel tacos and Lebanese pizza. Holy goodness, you need this place in your life. Already planning my next trip back.<//Text>

Mike's hummus is outstanding.<//text><Pictures>None</Pictures><response>None</response>< gmap_id>

<user_id>109942804449959820925< /user_id><username>Kyle Field<//username>< Date>
1474911139321</Date>
<Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
Tasty Lebanese food at reasonable prices in an area that's typically a vacuum when it come to Mediterranean food.

We were originally very excited to learn that there was a new Mediterranean eatery in town and our excitement was confirmed when we came here to eat. The hummus here is packed with flavor and has a smooth but chunky texture. The flavors explode in your mouth at first bite with a delicious creaminess that just brings it all together.
The falafel is crispy and packed with flavor...just a delicious bite of goodness if you ask me. This flavor only gets better when wrapped up into a sandwich where it gets to hang out with all sorts of crunchy, creamy friends that take it to a new level.
Shwarma - my wife loves the chicken schwarma here and without fail orders something with it. It's most, flavorful and fresh, getting carved right off the grill just a few feet away. Tasty!

Cons:
The menu is a bit kludgy. It's hard to figure out what you're actually ordering...and not just because the names aren't familiar. What's written on the board isn't the same as what's on the printed menus and it's just not clear what is what. It would be great if this were cleaned up a bit - especially considering that most people who visit aren't familiar with traditional Lebanese food.
The bread isn't super fresh. I have to admit - I'm a bread fan. I love pita, naan, flatbread...any bread and fresh is a huge factor when it comes to bread. If the bread were made in house or maybe even just a fluffier pita, it would really kick the food here up a few notches.<//Review>

PINCH $20 cash special on Thursdays!! Was delicious and so happy to hear about it!

‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî

So happy this moved into the neighborhood! Was very skeptical when I found on eater that this moved in. Seemed interesting but would it be worth a second visit? It absolutely is. Went for Sunday brunch. Was surprised at how delicious and flavorful everything is! Small, nicely decorated place in LA - look for a building with white bricks!  Inside felt spacious due to the high ceiling.

Poultry and Mushroom Porridge - very delicious porridge made from veggie stock.  Soy glazed chicken was delicious and the extra hibiscus shiso grilled egg ($2) was a great addition.

Eggs Meurrette + Black Sweet Rice - a crispy black rice pilaf with some beans in it topped with crispy shallots.  The dish next to it had the soft eggs (a little runnier than poached) in the ride wine sauce.  Very delicious since the sauce was sweet but also was balanced by the fat.

Would come again!</text>

< review>
I was a skeptic when my colleague asked us to have porridge for dinner (and a newb to Filipino food to be fair). Our dinner was a pleasant surprise! The table ordered all the sides and bowls of their shortribs special and chicken dish... both were delicious. Their puffs (naked)... Think of them like breadsticks, but better. I bought a box of the rice flour they make them with on the way out in the hopes that I could ever try and match it. The consistency of the porridge was more like a risotto... But not cheesy. Just tasty. And finally, there was a brown butter miso dessert that the table wished we hadn't opted to share. Utterly wonderful and if I could go back and order only one thing, it would be a toss up between that amazing bread and the dessert. Finally, the staff was wonderful, gracious, and used to being asked about the food. The owner/head chef was delightful. Seating is limited and available parking is on the street only, so it's worth making a reservation and the trip!< /review>

< Review>
Just moved back in town and was looking for a new Chinese food place so after having read some raving reviews on here I thought I would give it a shot. I placed the my to go order online which indicated it would take about 15 minutes, however, after having arrived in about 20 minutes the order was not ready and I had to wait but I was understanding considering it was Christmas Eve. I had ordered the house fried rice, orange chicken, beef and broccoli, and the cream cheese wontons. I found the overall price of $37.45 to be a bit on the higher side but gave it the benefit of the doubt because unlike other places I‚Äôve ordered from before where multiple sizes were an option China Fusion did not offer a small, medium, or large option so I thought that perhaps the portions would have been larger. Upon arrival at home I felt the portions were rather small for the price, and after having waited I would have expected our food to still be hot/warm but it was almost cold. I only live 7 minutes away so this leads me to believe that perhaps the food was not made as fresh as I would have hoped. The orange chicken and beef and broccoli was good. The cream cheese wontons and house fried rice lacked flavor and there were a lot of fatty chicken pieces in the rice. Sadly I will be seeking another Chinese food place to call home.</Review>

<review>This is my kind of place! I love restaurants with fixed price lunch specials and this one has a huge selection between $8 and $9. For our family of 4, we got the Orange Chicken, Moo goo gai pan, Shrimp & Broccoli and an order of potstickers.  When the dust settled, we were all stuffed and took home a large styro full of food.  The Orange Chicken is more what I consider classic sweet and sour and was super yummy.  The Moo goo had nice tender chicken and the sauce was flavorful enough, but I don't love Moo goo in general, so it was as good as it can be. I chose the Shrimp & Broccoli figuring it may just have a beefy sauce as typical with Beef & Broccoli, but was pleasantly surprised that it had a nice "shrimpiness" to it.  The potstickers were fried to perfection.  They also had Fanta Orange on tap and their drink price is a buck, so it was as good as it gets!  Nothing tastes more delicious than good value :)  We travel to Carlsbad every few years and this may have earned a place in the re-visit list.< /review>< pictures>

I do a lot of my own service because of bad and poor experiences in the past.  The experience I have had at Lodi CDJR is one just as bad if not worse.  I originally took my Jeep in on 8/6/16 to have the air bag recall performed and to get an estimate for a check engine light.  (smog related).  For my jeep when it comes to smog issue, I want factory parts. Lodi CDJR furnishes a courtesy shuttle. (I need to rely on the courtesy vehicle because my Jeep is our only vehicle)  My Jeep was ready that day for pickup  (parts were ordered and I needed the vehicle ). I asked if the shuttle could pick me up. I was asked what time. I said 1 o'clock. They agreed.  I waited until 2:30 to call the dealer asking where my ride was. I was told they were just leaving.  I brought my Jeep in first thing Monday morning and got a ride home on the shuttle. At around 11:30 I was called saying my Jeep was ready.  I said I needed a ride. I was told they do not have anyone available at this time. They would call me when they did.  I waited until almost 3:30. I called the dealership back. I was told they just found someone that could get me. Then I waited another 45 minutes for the ride.  When I picked up my Jeep my front passenger door window was down about 4 inches and would not go up or down. Ended up being a repair I would have to do. They would not repair unless I paid to have it repaired.  All the windows were up when I left my vehicle that morning. My thought  is someone slammed the door that broke the cable on the regulator. The next day I tried no less than 6 times to call Robert, the service manager, who was always busy or not in. The operator told me I needed to leave  him a voice mail with my name and number and he would call me back. I left Robert  a voice mail with my name and number on 8/9/16 . I AM STILL WAITING AND IT IS MONDAY THE 15TH. Robert don't waste my time now with a phone call. My Jeep is a 2003 with low miles and very clean, at no time during any of the work being done was my seat covered with plastic to protect the vehicle seat from the dirty clothes of the mechanics.  My Jeep now gets 13.7 miles per gallon, it was getting 18.2 miles per gallon before they worked on it.  I will never buy, recommend or have any work done on any of my vehicles at Lodi CDJR.  I was thinking of buying a new Grand Cherokee Jeep and pass this one to one of my grand kids. If I do it will not be from this dealership.
For the mileage problem I found the cover from the air cleaner to the top of the fuel injection installed wrong. I reinstalled the cover and retrained the computer and now I have my good mileage back.  It is really to bad when the customer has to repair what the professionals work on. My personal recommendation use caution and think twice before dealing with Lodi CDJR.</Review>
